name:Pâ€iâ€dâ€aâ€nâ€0â€0â€8
info:Business Double Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:The room is not big, but it is enough. Generally, the first room on each floor starting with 01 has a bathtub. The room is clean and the service is good. I used to stay in Shandong Building on Maanshan Road. This is my first time staying in Qingzhao Hotel in Zhangqiu. It is generally good. Breakfast is not expensive, only a few dozen yuan. It may be the Qingming Festival holiday. Obviously, the kitchen can't keep up. Most people eat at 8.30-9.30 in the morning. This time, there is basically no food in the morning meal. The evening buffet is much worse. Three slices of salmon can only be served per person, one person for three slices. Five or six people in the evening that day It was gone at 7 o'clock. I was really impressed. Ctrip and Dianping said that this hotel is five-star or five-diamond, but it should be a four-star at best. Of course, the price is much lower, 48 for breakfast and 99 for dinner, but the breakfast is okay, there is basically nothing to eat for dinner, and the replenishment is slow. In addition, I booked five rooms in this hotel, which is seven or eight kilometers away from the center of Zhangqiu for a quiet place. I also thought there was a swimming pool, but I really thought too much. First, it is close to Jingshi Road, second, there is no swimming pool, and third, there is nothing around. In addition to going to the hotel for meals, you can only drive to the university town. Other things are okay, overall it is worth the discounted price, I hope it will get better and better!
